Bhāskara Bhagavadāśayānusaraṇabhāsya
Additional Remark
bhāskarabhāṣyasya prathamapṛṣṭhasya dve vākye
ānandajayatīrthakṛtagītāṭīkāyā uddhṛte 
tayoḥ sāhāyyena bhāskarakṛtagītābhāṣyasya
luptaprathamapṛṣṭhasya viṣayonumātuṃ śakyate 
te vākye
 śāstraprayojanābhidhāne prastute 'vatāraprayojanābhidhānam asaṃgatam 
 jñānakarmasamuccayasādhyatvān mokṣasya tatpratipādanāya gītārambhe na dharmādipratipādanārtham 
tadarthānāṃ manvādidharmaśāstrāṇāṃ sanakādiyogaśāstrāṇāṃ ca pratikālaṃ vidyamānatvāt 
jayatīrthaṭīkāyām yad āha bhāskara iti vākyād anantaram upalabhete ime vākye 
tatra prathamaṃ vākyaṃ ṣaṣṭhe pṛṣṭhe dvitīyaṃ vākyaṃ navame pṛṣṭhe  p 
śrībhagavadgītāyā
bhagavadbhāskarakṛtabhagavadāśayānusaraṇābhidhānabhāṣyam 
idaṃ hi triṣu lokeṣu mahajjñānaṃ
pratiṣṭitam 
vistaraiś ca samāsaiś ca dhāryate yad dvijātibhiḥ 
yodhīte bhārata puṇyaṃ brāhmaṇo niyatavrataḥ 
śrāvayec ca mahāpuṇyaṃ tasya dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ 
taponiyamam āsthāya kṛtam etan maharṣiṇā 
tasmān niyamasaṃyuktair adhyeyaṃ brāhmaṇair idam 
kṛṣṇaproktam imāṃ puṇyāṃ bhāratīm uttamāṃ kathām 
śrāvayiṣyanti ye viprā ye ca śroṣyanti mānavāḥ 
ityevamādau śrāvayiṣyanti ityatra vipragrahaṇād
dvijātīnām evādhyayane śravaṇe cādhikāro darśitaḥ 
itareṣāṃ tu ye tu śrośyanti mānavā iti mānavagrahaṇāc chravaṇa
evādhikāraḥ śāstravirodhāc cādhyayane nādhikāraḥ 
tathā coktaṃ śukotpattau
sarvas taratu durgāṇi sarvo bhadrāṇi paśyatu 
śrāvayec caturo varṇān kṛtvā brāhmaṇam agrataḥ

tāś ca parigaṇayann āha
bhavān bhīṣmaś ca karṇaś ca kṛpaḥ śalyo jayadrathaḥ 
aśvatthāmā vikarṇaś ca saumadattiś ca vīryavān  BhG 
na kevalam ete yāvat
anye 'pi bahavaḥ śūrā madarthe tyaktajīvitāḥ 
nānāśastrapraharaṇā nānāyuddhaviśāradāḥ  BhG 
nānāprakārāṇi cakrāsimuśalagadāprabhṛtīni śastrāṇi

nirūpayann āha
aparyāptaṃ tad asmākaṃ balaṃ bhīmābhirakṣitam 
paryāptaṃ tv idam eteṣāṃ balaṃ bhīṣmābhirakṣitam  BhG 
asmākaṃ yathānirdiṣṭasaṃhatānāṃ tatpāṇḍavabalam
aparyāptam asamartham abhibhavitum yato bhīmābhirakṣitam
bhīmasenena pradhānabhūtena guptam 
sa ca bhīmo bhīṣmāpekṣayā kiñcin nyūnatara ity abhiprāyaḥ 
idaṃ tv asmākaṃ balam eteṣāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ paryāptam
abhibhavāya vināśane samartham ity arthaḥ yato bhīṣmābhirakṣitam 
bhīṣmas tv anekaśastrāstrapārago nirjitānekamahāsamara ityāśayaḥ

pradhānanirdeśaparyojanam āha

yathābhāgam

sāmānyanader viśeṣanadiḥ karma

hantavyā iti 
kathaṃ hi bhrātrādivadhād evādharmo 'smān na
bhajata iti hatvā pāpam āśrayed iti 
atrāpiśabdena nyāye
bhinnakartṛkatā vāstavena tu nāsti

tataś ca eva hanti tenaiva kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ syād ity ekaḥ kartā   
evaṃ bhrātrādivadhāśaṅkāviklavam abhidhāya
tadabhiprāyāviṣkaraṇāyāha 
tasmān nārhā vayaṃ hantuṃ dhārtarāṣṭrān svabandhavān 
svajanaṃ hi kathaṃ hatvā sukhinaḥ syāma mādhava  BhG 
yasmād dhārtarāṣṭrahananāt prītir nāsti pratyutādharmaḥ
tasmāt tān svajanavargān hantuṃ vayaṃ nārhāḥ 
svajanaṃ hi hatvā kathaṃ sukhino bhavema 
dharmabahiṣkṛtānām etadācāraṇam ityabhyiprāyaḥ

kulakṣayakṛtaṃ doṣaṃ prapaśyadbhir janārdana  BhG

dvividhaṃ phalam anvayanibandhanaṃ tātparyasamadhigamyaṃ ca

padārthasaṃsargo hi vākyārthaḥ 
na punar yāgānuṣṭhānena jñānayogyatāṃ kuryād iti
kasyacit padasya tātparyo dṛśyate 
padārthapūrvakaś ca vākyārtho jñāne nimittam iti sthitiḥ 
na ca puruṣecchāvaśād vākyasya nārthāntaram ākṣipati 
ye hi śrūyamāṇam artham anādṛtya vākyasyārthāntaraṃ kalpayanti
ta eva sutarām avipaścito na mīmāṃsakā
ye śabdapramāṇavṛttaṃ
bruvate śamadamādayo yāgānuṣṭhānasādhyā iti 
kiṃ tarhi  śānto dānta uparataḥ

na buddhibhedaṃ janayed ajñānām ity ajñagrahaṇaṃ jñāpakam

yataḥ sannyāsī yogam āsādya brahma pratipadyate nānyathā 
ato yogasya yad uktaṃ viśiṣṭatvaṃ tad upapannam ity upasaṃharati

kiṃ tad brahma kim adhyātmaṃ kiṃ karma puruṣottama

iti

śeṣaṃ gatārtham   
śukrakṛṣṇe gatī hy ete jagataḥ śāśvate mate 
ekayā yāty anāvṛttim anyayāvartate punaḥ  BhG 
śukleti  ete ca gatī śuklakṛṣṇe jagataḥ 
śāśvate mate
vedoktatvāt  ekayā yāty anāvṛttim anyayāvartate punar iti 
arthasya punar vacanaṃ nigamanam   
mārgadvayābhijñaḥ kevalaṃ karma nārabhate samuccayārtham eva yatate
niḥśreyasārthatvād iti darśayitum āha 
naite sṛtī pārtha jānan yogī muhyati kaścana 
tasmāt sarveṣu kāleṣu yogayukto bhavārjuna  BhG 
naita iti   
tad etad adhyāyoktaṃ jñānam anyanindayā stūyate 
śraddhālavaḥ katham atrābhiyuktā bhaveyur iti

śruṇu tataḥ phalam 
śubhāśubhaphalair evaṃ mokṣyase karmabandhanaiḥ 
sannyāsayogayuktātmā vimukto mām upaiṣyasi  BhG 
śubheti  śubhāśubhāni phalāni yeṣāṃ karmabandhanānām 
karmāṇy eva bandhanāni 
tair vimucyase 
vimuktaś ca sannyāsayogayuktātmā 
sannyāsaḥ kṛtānāṃ karmaṇāṃ
brahmaṇi samarpaṇam  tad eva
p 
kartṛkarmaphalaṃ cety abhedabhāvanā yogaḥ 
tābhyāṃ yukta ātmā
yasyāsau sannyāsayogayukt
ātmā mām upeṣyasi   
nanu yas tvayi samarpaṇaṃ karoti sa eva cet tvām upaiti
rāgādimāṃs tarhi bhavān yathā loke rājā bhajamānasyopakaroti
netarasyety āśaṅkyāha 
samohaṃ sarvabhūteṣu na me dveṣyo 'sti na priyaḥ 
ye bhajanti tu māṃ bhaktyā mayi te teṣu cāpy aham  BhG 
samoham iti 
samohaṃ sarvabhūteṣu na me rāgadveṣau  yo bhaktyā
māṃ bhajate tasyānugrahaṃ kartuṃ mama svabhāvaḥ yathāgniḥ
samyag bhajamānasya śītādyapanodaṃ karoti netarasya  ato ye
bhajanti tu bhaktyā sevante mām
āśrayante teṣv ahaṃ varte 
nātra rāgadveṣau kāraṇam  api tu
prāṇikarmānurūpaphalapradarśanenāgnivadanugṛhṇāmīty
abhiprāyaḥ   
idānīṃ vṛttādinirākaraṇenāpi bhagavadāśrayaṇastutyartham
arthavādakathanaṃ kriyate 
vṛttam apy atra tantram ity āha 
api cet sudurācāro bhajate mām ananyabhāk 
sādhur eva sa mantavyaḥ samyag vyavasito hi saḥ  BhG 
apīti  suṣṭhu bhṛśaṃ ced durācāraḥ so 'pi sādhur eva
mantavyaḥ  kasmāt 
samyag vyavasitaḥ suniścitabuddhiḥ sanmārgam
āsthito yataḥ 
hiśabdo hetau

 ṭi  pāpakṣayāt

bhaktaḥ praṇaśyatīti

prakrāntaṃ tatra śraddhābhaktibhyāṃ
bhagavadvyapāśrayaṇaprarovanārtham
apy arthavādam āha 
māṃ hi pārtha vyapāśritya ye 'pi syuḥ pāpayonayaḥ 
striyo vaiśyās tathā śūdrās te 'pi yānti parāṃ gatim  BhG 
mām iti  he pārtha māṃ vyapāśritya viśeṣeṇa śaraṇatvenāśritya
ye 'pi pāpayonayo bhavanti 
pāpād yonir janma yeṣāṃ te pāpayonayaḥ

paramāṃ

sambhāvyate
